*Grade 1 Maths — March Quiz*
_2106 questions (1606 new + 500 revision)_

*Q1.* 🎒 Diya packs 4 bags with 3 grapes in each bag. How many grapes altogether?
A) 13
B) 11
C) 7
D) 12
✅ *Answer:* D) 12
💡 4 groups of 3 = 12 grapes.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q2.* 🎒 Sia packs 5 bags with 6 butterflies in each bag. How many butterflies altogether?
A) 30
B) 11
C) 29
D) 31
✅ *Answer:* A) 30
💡 5 groups of 6 = 30 butterflies.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q3.* 🍪 There were 18 mangoes. Kiara ate 12. How many mangoes left?
A) 18
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
✅ *Answer:* C) 6
💡 18 - 12 = 6 mangoes left.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q4.* 📉 Arranged greatest → smallest, which comes FIRST? 69, 30, 52
A) 70
B) 30
C) 52
D) 69
✅ *Answer:* D) 69
💡 Descending order starts with 69.

*Q2101.* 💳 Sara buys a biscuit for ₹4 and pays with a ₹10 note. How much change?
A) ₹8
B) ₹5
C) ₹6
D) ₹7
✅ *Answer:* C) ₹6
💡 ₹10 - ₹4 = ₹6.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q2102.* 🎒 Pari packs 6 bags with 6 butterflies in each bag. How many butterflies altogether?
A) 37
B) 36
C) 12
D) 35
✅ *Answer:* B) 36
💡 6 groups of 6 = 36 butterflies.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q2103.* 🧺 Kabya makes 5 equal groups with 6 fish in each. How many fish in all?
A) 29
B) 11
C) 30
D) 31
✅ *Answer:* C) 30
💡 5 groups of 6 = 30 fish.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q2104.* 🎒 Sara packs 4 bags with 3 butterflies in each bag. How many butterflies altogether?
A) 7
B) 12
C) 11
D) 13
✅ *Answer:* B) 12
💡 4 groups of 3 = 12 butterflies.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q2105.* 🐜 Which is the SMALLEST? 20, 1, 29, 13
A) 20
B) 1
C) 29
D) 13
✅ *Answer:* B) 1
💡 1 is the smallest.

*Q2106.* 🧺 Kiara makes 3 equal groups with 2 crayons in each. How many crayons in all?
A) 5
B) 6
C) 8
D) 7
✅ *Answer:* B) 6
💡 3 groups of 2 = 6 crayons.
